Source Code

These source-code files were from the printout at the MIT Museum, with many thanks to Deborah Douglas, the Museum's Curator of Science and Technology, for releasing it to us. The printout was digitally photographed by Paul Fjeld. A team of volunteers transcribed the source code manually from these images or, where appropriate, modified already-transcribed but similar source Luminary 131 (Apollo 13) source code to agree with the images from the printout. Note that the page images presented online are of reduced quality, and that higher-quality images are available. Report any conversion errors or legibility problems in page images to info@sandroid.org. Notations on the program listing read, in part:

	GAP:  ASSEMBLE REVISION 001 OF AGC PROGRAM LMY99 BY NASA 2021112-061
	20'35 OCT. 28,1968
Note that the date is the date of the printout, not the date of the program revision.

021119,000004:                                                                                                  #  Purpose:      Part of the source code for Luminary 1A build 099.

021127,000012:                                                                                                  #                2009-06-05 RSB  Corrected a typos.
021128,000013:                                                                                                  #                2009-06-06 RSB  Added a missing instruction, and a block
021129,000014:                                                                                                  #                                of 3 missing instructions.
021130,000015:                                                                                                  #                2009-06-07 RSB  Fixed a misprint.
021131,000016:                                                                                                  #                2009-06-07 RSB  Changed the construct "2DEC E-6 B12" 
021132,000017:                                                                                                  #                                (which isn't legal in yaYUL) to
021133,000018:                                                                                                  #                                "2DEC 1.0 E-6 B12".
021134,000019:                                                                                                  #                2011-05-07 JL   Removed workarounds.

021138,000023:                                                                                                  #  was performed by Paul Fjeld, and arranged for by Deborah Douglas of
021139,000024:                                                                                                  #  the Museum.  Many thanks to both.  The images (with suitable reduction

021146,000031:                                                                                                  #  Notations on the hardcopy document read, in part:
021147,000032: 
021148,000033:                                                                                                  #        Assemble revision 001 of AGC program LMY99 by NASA 2021112-61
021149,000034:                                                                                                  #        16:27 JULY 14, 1969 
021150,000035: 
021151,000036:                                                                                                  #  Page 492
021152,000037:                                                                                                  #  RENDEZVOUS NAVIGATION PROGRAM 20
021153,000038: 
021154,000039:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM DESCRIPTION
021155,000040: 
021156,000041:                                                                                                  #        MOD NO -- 2
021157,000042:                                                                                                  #        BY P. VOLANTE
021158,000043: 
021159,000044:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION
021160,000045: 
021161,000046:                                                                                                  #        THE PURPOSE OF THIS PROGRAM IS TO CONTROL THE RENDEZVOUS RADAR FROM
021162,000047:                                                                                                  #        STARTUP THROUGH ACQUISITION AND LOCKON TO THE CSM AND TO UPDATE EITHER 
021163,000048:                                                                                                  #        THE LM OR CSM STATE VECTOR (AS SPECIFIED BY THE ASTRONAUT BY DSKY ENTRY)
021164,000049:                                                                                                  #        ON THE BASIS OF THE RR TRACKING DATA.
021165,000050: 
021166,000051:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE --
021167,000052: 
021168,000053:                                                                                                  #        ASTRONAUT REQUEST THROUGH DSKY V37E20E
021169,000054: 
021170,000055:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED
021171,000056: 
021172,000057:                                                                                                  #        R02BOTH (IMU STATUS CHECK)                      FLAGUP
021173,000058:                                                                                                  #        GOFLASH (PINBALL-DISPLAY)                       FLAGDOWN
021174,000059:                                                                                                  #        R23LEM  (MANUAL ACQUISITION)                    BANKCALL
021175,000060:                                                                                                  #        LS201   (LOS DETERMINATION)                     TASKOVER
021176,000061:                                                                                                  #        LS202   (RANGE LIMIT TEST)
021177,000062:                                                                                                  #        R61LEM  (PREFERRED TRACKING ATTITUDE)
021178,000063:                                                                                                  #        R21LEM  (RR DESIGNATE)                          ENDOFJOB
021179,000064:                                                                                                  #        R22LEM  (DATA READ)                             GOPERF1
021180,000065:                                                                                                  #        R31LEM  (RENDEZVOUS PARAMETER DISPLAY)  
021181,000066:                                                                                                  #        PRIOLARM (PRIORITY DISPLAY)
021182,000067: 
021183,000068:                                                                                                  #  NORMAL EXIT MODES --
021184,000069: 
021185,000070:                                                                                                  #        P20 MAY BE TERMINATED IN TWO WAYS -- ASTRONAUT SELECTION OF IDLING
021186,000071:                                                                                                  #        PROGRAM (P00) BY KEYING V37E00E OR BY KEYING IN V56E
021187,000072: 
021188,000073:                                                                                                  #  ALARM OR ABORT EXIT MODES --
021189,000074: 
021190,000075:                                                                                                  #        RANGE GREATER THAN 400 NM DISPLAY
021191,000076: 
021192,000077:                                                                                                  #  OUTPUT
021193,000078: 
021194,000079:                                                                                                  #        TRKMKCNT = NO OF RENDEZVOUS TRACKING MARKS TAKEN (COUNTER)
021195,000080: 
021196,000081:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED
021197,000082: 
021198,000083:                                                                                                  #  FLAGS SET + RESET
021199,000084: 
021200,000085:                                                                                                  #        SRCHOPT, RNDVZFLG, ACMODFLG, VEHUPFLG, UPDATFLG, TRACKFLG
021201,000086: 
021202,000087:                                                                                                  #  DEBRIS
021203,000088: 
021204,000089:                                                                                                  #        CENTRALS -- A,Q,L
021205,000090: 
021206,000091: 25,2062  30,2000                                  SBANK=   LOWSUPER                              #  FOR LOW 2CADR'S.
021207,000092:

021209,000094: 24,2000                                           SETLOC   P20S

021621,000506:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM DESCRIPTION
021622,000507: 
021623,000508:                                                                                                  #        PREFERRED TRACKING ATTITUDE PROGRAM P25
021624,000509:                                                                                                  #        MOD NO -- 3
021625,000510:                                                                                                  #        BY P. VOLANTE
021626,000511: 
021627,000512:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION
021628,000513: 
021629,000514:                                                                                                  #        THE PURPOSE OF THIS PROGRAM IS TO COMPUTE THE PREFERRED TRACKING
021630,000515:                                                                                                  #        ATTITUDE OF THE LM TO CONTINUOUSLY POINT THE LM TRTACKING BEACON AT THE
021631,000516:                                                                                                  #        CSM AND TO PERFORM THE MANEUVER TO THE PREFERRED TRACKING ATTITUDE AND
021632,000517:                                                                                                  #        CONTINUOUSLY MAINTAIN THIS ATTITUDE WITHIN PRESCRIBED LIMITS.
021633,000518: 
021634,000519:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE --
021635,000520: 
021636,000521:                                                                                                  #        ASTRONAUT REQUEST THROUGH DSKY V37E25E
021637,000522:

021639,000524: 
021640,000525:                                                                                                  #        BANKCALL                                        FLAGUP

021642,000527:                                                                                                  #        R61LEM  (PREF TRK ATT ROUT)                     WAITLIST
021643,000528:                                                                                                  #        TASKOVER                                        FINDVAC
021644,000529: 
021645,000530:                                                                                                  #  NORMAL EXIT MODES --

021647,000532:                                                                                                  #        P25 MAY BE TERMINATED IN TWO WAYS -- ASTRONAUT SELECTION OF IDLING
021648,000533:                                                                                                  #        PROGRAM (P00) BY KEYING V37E00E OR BY KEYING IN V56E

021923,000808: 
021924,000809:                                                                                                  #  Page 508
021925,000810:                                                                                                  #  RR DESIGNATE ROUTINE (R21LEM)
021926,000811:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM DESCRIPTION
021927,000812: 
021928,000813:                                                                                                  #        MOD NO -- 2
021929,000814:                                                                                                  #        BY P. VOLANTE
021930,000815: 
021931,000816:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION
021932,000817: 
021933,000818:                                                                                                  #        TO POINT THE RENDEZVOUS RADAR AT THE CSM UNTIL AUTOMATIC ACQUISITION
021934,000819:                                                                                                  #        OF THE CSM IS ACCOMPLISHED BY THE RADAR.  ROUTINE IS CALLED BY P20.
021935,000820: 
021936,000821:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE --
021937,000822: 
021938,000823:                                                                                                  #        TC      BANKCALL
021939,000824:                                                                                                  #        CADR    R21LEM
021940,000825: 
021941,000826:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED --
021942,000827: 
021943,000828:                                                                                                  #        FINDVAC         FLAGUP          ENDOFJOB        PRIOLARM
021944,000829:                                                                                                  #        NOVAC           INTPRET         LPS20.1         PHASCHNG
021945,000830:                                                                                                  #        WAITLIST        JOBSLEEP        JOBWAKE         FLAGDOWN
021946,000831:                                                                                                  #        TASKOVER        BANKCALL        RADSTALL        RRDESSM
021947,000832: 
021948,000833:                                                                                                  #  NORMAL EXIT MODES
021949,000834:                                                                                                  #        
021950,000835:                                                                                                  #        WHEN LOCK-ON IS ACHIEVED, BRANCH WILL BE TO P20 WHERE R22 (DATA READ
021951,000836:                                                                                                  #        WILL BE SELECTED OR A NEED FOR A MANEUVER (BRANCH TO P20LEMA)
021952,000837: 
021953,000838:                                                                                                  #  ALARM OR ABORT EXIT MODES --
021954,000839: 
021955,000840:                                                                                                  #        PRIORITY ALARM 503 WHEN LOCK-ON HASN'T BEEN ACHIEVED AFTER 30SECS --
021956,000841:                                                                                                  #        THIS REQUIRES ASTRONAUT INTERFACE: SELECTION OF SEARCH OPTION OF
021957,000842:                                                                                                  #        ACQUISITION
021958,000843: 
021959,000844:                                                                                                  #  OUTPUT
021960,000845: 
021961,000846:                                                                                                  #        SEE LPS20.1, RRDESSM
021962,000847: 
021963,000848:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED
021964,000849: 
021965,000850:                                                                                                  #        RRTARGET, RADMODES ARE USED BY LPS20.1 AND RRDESSM
021966,000851: 
021967,000852:                                                                                                  #  FLAGS SET + RESET
021968,000853: 
021969,000854:                                                                                                  #        LOSCMFLG        LOKONSW
021970,000855: 
021971,000856:                                                                                                  #  DEBRIS
021972,000857: 
021973,000858:                                                                                                  #        SEE LPS20.1, RRSESSM
021974,000859: 
021975,000860: 24,2674  E7,1456                                  EBANK=   LOSCOUNT                              
021976,000861: 24,2674                                           COUNT*   $$/R21                                
021977,000862: 24,2674           44736        R21LEM             CS       BIT14                                 #  REMOVE RR SELF TRACK ENABLE
021978,000863: 24,2675           00006                           EXTEND

022150,001035:                                                                                                  #  MANUAL ACQUISITION ROUTINE R23LEM
022151,001036:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM DESCRIPTION
022152,001037: 
022153,001038:                                                                                                  #        MOD NO -- 2
022154,001039:                                                                                                  #        BY P. VOLANTE
022155,001040: 
022156,001041:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION
022157,001042: 
022158,001043:                                                                                                  #        TO ACQUIRE THE CSM BY MANUAL OPERATION OF THE RENDEZVOUS RADAR
022159,001044: 
022160,001045:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE --
022161,001046: 
022162,001047:                                                                                                  #        TC      R23LEM
022163,001048: 
022164,001049:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED
022165,001050: 
022166,001051:                                                                                                  #        BANKCALL        R61LEM
022167,001052:                                                                                                  #        SETMINDB        GOPERF1
022168,001053: 
022169,001054:                                                                                                  #  NORMAL EXIT MODES --
022170,001055: 
022171,001056:                                                                                                  #        IN RESPONSE TO THE GOPERF1,     SELECTION OF ENTER WILL RECYCLE R23
022172,001057:                                                                                                  #                                        SELECTION OF PROC WILL CONTINUE R23
022173,001058:                                                                                                  #                                        SELECTION OF TERM WILL TERMINATE R23 + P20
022174,001059: 
022175,001060:                                                                                                  #  ALARM OR ABORT EXIT MODES --
022176,001061: 
022177,001062:                                                                                                  #        SEE NORMAL EXIT MODES ABOVE
022178,001063: 
022179,001064:                                                                                                  #  OUTPUT
022180,001065: 
022181,001066:                                                                                                  #        N.A.
022182,001067: 
022183,001068:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED --
022184,001069: 
022185,001070:                                                                                                  #        ACMODFLG MUST BE SET TO 1 (MANUAL MODE)
022186,001071: 
022187,001072: 24,3135     1143                                  EBANK=   GENRET                                
022188,001073: 24,3135                                           COUNT*   $$/R23                                
022189,001074: 24,3135           05504        R23LEM             TC       UPFLAG                                #  SET NO ANGLE MONITOR FLAG
022190,001075: 24,3136           00126                           ADRES    NORRMON                               
022191,001076: 24,3137           00004                           INHINT                                         
022192,001077: 24,3140           04674                           TC       IBNKCALL                              #  SELECT MINIMUM DEADBAND
022193,001078: 24,3141           40140                           CADR     SETMINDB                              
022194,001079: 24,3142           00003                           RELINT                                         
022195,001080: 24,3143           34736        R23LEM1            CAF      BIT14                                 #  ENABLE TRACKER
022196,001081: 24,3144           00006                           EXTEND                                         
022197,001082: 24,3145           05012                           WOR      CHAN12                                
022198,001083: 24,3146           33205                           CAF      OCT205                                
022199,001084: 24,3147           04616                           TC       BANKCALL                              
022200,001085: 24,3150           20623                           CADR     GOPERF1                               
022201,001086: 24,3151           03176                           TC       R23LEM2                               #  TERMINATE
022202,001087: 24,3152           03154                           TC       R23LEM11                              #  PROCEDE
022203,001088: 24,3153           03201                           TC       R23LEM3                               #  ENTER -- DO ANOTHER MANEUVER
022204,001089: 24,3154           00004        R23LEM11           INHINT

022233,001118:                                                                                                  #  Page 515
022234,001119:                                                                                                  #  SEARCH ROUTINE R24LEM
022235,001120:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM DESCRIPTION
022236,001121: 
022237,001122:                                                                                                  #        MOD NO -- 2
022238,001123:                                                                                                  #        BY P. VOLANTE
022239,001124: 
022240,001125:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION
022241,001126: 
022242,001127:                                                                                                  #        TO ACQUIRE THE CSM BY A SEARCH PATTERN WHEN THE RENDEZVOUS RADAR HAS
022243,001128:                                                                                                  #        FAILED TO ACQUIRE TEH CSM IN THE AUTOMATIC TRACKING MODE AND TO ALLOW
022244,001129:                                                                                                  #        THE ASTRONAUT TO CONFIRM THAT REACQUISITION HAS NOT BEEN IN SIDELOBE.
022245,001130: 
022246,001131:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE
022247,001132: 
022248,001133:                                                                                                  #        CAF     PRIONN
022249,001134:                                                                                                  #        TC      FINDVAC
022250,001135:                                                                                                  #        EBANK=  DATAGOOD
022251,001136:                                                                                                  #        2CADR   R24LEM
022252,001137: 
022253,001138:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED
022254,001139: 
022255,001140:                                                                                                  #        FLAGUP          FLAGDOWN        BANKCALL
022256,001141:                                                                                                  #        R61LEM          GOFLASHR        FINDVAC
022257,001142:                                                                                                  #        ENDOFJOB        NOVAC           LSR24.1
022258,001143: 
022259,001144:                                                                                                  #  NORMAL EXIT MODES --
022260,001145: 
022261,001146:                                                                                                  #        ASTRONAUT RESPONSE TO DISPLAY OF OMEGA AND DATAGOOD.  HE CAN EITHER
022262,001147:                                                                                                  #        REJECT BY TERMINATING (SEARCH OPTION AND RESELECTING P20) OR ACCEPT BY
022263,001148:                                                                                                  #        PROCEEDING (EXIT ROUTINE AND RETURN TO AUTO MODE IN P20)
022264,001149: 
022265,001150:                                                                                                  #  ALARM OR ABORT EXIT MODES --
022266,001151: 
022267,001152:                                                                                                  #        SEE NORMAL EXIT MODES ABOVE
022268,001153: 
022269,001154:                                                                                                  #  OUTPUT --
022270,001155: 
022271,001156:                                                                                                  #        SEE OUTPUT FROM LSR24.1 + R61LEM
022272,001157: 
022273,001158:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED
022274,001159: 
022275,001160:                                                                                                  #        SET INPUT FOR LSR24.1
022276,001161: 
022277,001162:                                                                                                  #  FLAGS SET + RESET
022278,001163: 
022279,001164:                                                                                                  #        SRCHOPT, ACMODFLG
022280,001165: 
022281,001166: 24,3206  E7,1733                                  EBANK=   DATAGOOD                              
022282,001167: 24,3206                                           COUNT*   $$/R24

022286,001171: 24,3211           00041                           ADRES    LOSCMFLG                              #  SURE DODES DOESN'T GO TO R21
022287,001172: 24,3212           34755        R24LEM1            CAF      ZERO                                  
022288,001173: 24,3213           55733                           TS       DATAGOOD                              #  ZERO OUT DATA INDICATOR
022289,001174: 24,3214           55734                           TS       OMEGAD                                #  ZERO OMEGA DISPLAY REGS
022290,001175: 24,3215           55735                           TS       OMEGAD     +1                         #  ZERO OMEGA DISPLAY REGS

022342,001227: 24,3251           34755        R24LEM4            CAF      ZERO                                  #  ZERO OUT RADCADR (WHICH WAS SET BY

022557,001442: 
022558,001443:                                                                                                  #  Page 522
022559,001444:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME: RRLIMCHK
022560,001445: 
022561,001446:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION:
022562,001447: 
022563,001448:                                                                                                  #        RRLIMCHK CHECKS RR DESIRED GIMBAL ANGLES TO SEE IF THEY ARE WITHIN
022564,001449:                                                                                                  #        THE LIMITS OF THE CURRENT MODE.  INITIALLY THE DESIRED TRUNNION AND
022565,001450:                                                                                                  #        SHAFT ANGLES ARE STORED IN ITEMP1 AND ITEMP2.  THE CURRENT RR
022566,001451:                                                                                                  #        ANTENNAE MODE (RADMODES BIT 12) IS CHECKED WHICH IS = 0 FOR
022567,001452:                                                                                                  #        MODE 1 AND =1 FOR MODE 2.
022568,001453: 
022569,001454:                                                                                                  #        MODE 1 -- THE TRUNNION ANGLE IS CHECKED AT MAGSUB TO SEE IF IT IS
022570,001455:                                                                                                  #        BETWEEN -55 AND +55 DEGREES.  IF NOT, RETURN TO L +2.  IF WITHIN LIMITS,
022571,001456:                                                                                                  #        THE SHAFT ANGLE IS CHECKED TO SEE IF IT IS BETWEEN -70 AND +59 DEGREES.
022572,001457:                                                                                                  #        IF NOT, RETURN TO L +2.  IF IN LIMITS, RETURN TO L +3.
022573,001458: 
022574,001459:                                                                                                  #        MODE 2 -- THE SHAFT ANGLE IS CHECKED AT MAGSUB TO SEE IF IT IS
022575,001460:                                                                                                  #        BETWEEN -139 AND -25 DEGREES.  IF NOT, RETURN TO L +2.  IF WITHIN
022576,001461:                                                                                                  #        LIMITS, THE TRUNNION ANGLE IS CHECKED TO SEE IF IT IS BETWEEN +125
022577,001462:                                                                                                  #        AND -125 (+235) DEGREES.  IF NOT, RETURN TO L +2.  IF IN LIMITS, RETURN
022578,001463:                                                                                                  #        TO L +3.
022579,001464: 
022580,001465:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE:
022581,001466: 
022582,001467:                                                                                                  #        L  TC  RLIMCHK (WITH INTERRUPT INHIBITED)
022583,001468:                                                                                                  #        L  +1  ADRES  T,S  (DESIRED TRUNNION ANGLE ADDRESS)
022584,001469: 
022585,001470:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED:
022586,001471: 
022587,001472:                                                                                                  #        RADMODES, MODEA, MODEB (OR DESIRED TRUNNION AND SHAFT
022588,001473:                                                                                                  #        ANGLES ELSEWHERE IN CONSECUTIVE LOCATIONS -- UNSWITCHED ERASABLE OR
022589,001474:                                                                                                  #        CURRENT EBANK).
022590,001475: 
022591,001476:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED:   MAGSUB
022592,001477: 
022593,001478:                                                                                                  #  JOBS OR TASKS INITIATED:  NONE
022594,001479: 
022595,001480:                                                                                                  #  ALARMS:  NONE
022596,001481: 
022597,001482:                                                                                                  #  EXIT:         L + 2   (EITHER OR BOTH ANGLES NOT WITHIN LIMITS OF CURRENT MODE)
022598,001483:                                                                                                  #                L + 3   (BOTH ANGLES WITHIN LIMITS OF CURRENT MODE)
022599,001484:

022641,001526: 
022642,001527:                                                                                                  #  Page 524
022643,001528:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME: SETTRKF
022644,001529: 
022645,001530:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION:
022646,001531: 
022647,001532:                                                                                                  #        SETTRKF UPDATES THE TRACKER FAIL LAMP ON THE DSKY.
022648,001533:                                                                                                  #        INITIALLY THE LAMP TEST FLAG (IMODES33 BIT 1) IS CHECKED.
022649,001534:                                                                                                  #        IF A LAMP TEST IS IN PROGRESS, THE PROGRAM EXITS TO L +1.
022650,001535:                                                                                                  #        IF NO LAMP TEST THE FOLLOWING IS CHECKED SEQUENTIALLY:
022651,001536:                                                                                                  #                1) RR CDU'S BEING ZEROED, RR CDU OK, AND RR NOT IN
022652,001537:                                                                                                  #                   AUTO MODE (RADMODES BITS 13, 7, 2).
022653,001538:                                                                                                  #                2) LR VEL DATA FAIL AND NO LR POS DATA (RADMODES BITS
022654,001539:                                                                                                  #                   8,5)
022655,001540:                                                                                                  #                3) NO RR DATA (RADMODES BIT 4)
022656,001541:                                                                                                  #        THE ABSENCE OF ALL THREE SIMULTANEOUSLY IN (1), THE PRESENCE OF BOTH
022657,001542:                                                                                                  #        IN (2), AND THE PRESENCE OF (3) RESULTS IN EITHER THE TRACKER FAIL
022658,001543:                                                                                                  #        LAMP (DSPTAB +11D BIT 8) BEING TURNED OFF OR IS LEFT OFF.  THEREFORE, THE
022659,001544:                                                                                                  #        TRACKER FAIL LAMP IS TURN ON IF:
022660,001545:                                                                                                  #                A) RR CDU FAILED WITH RR IN AUTO MODE AND RR CDU'S NOT BEING ZEROED
022661,001546:                                                                                                  #                B) N SAMPLES OF LR DATA COULD NOT BE TAKEN IN 2N TRIES WITH
022662,001547:                                                                                                  #                   EITHER THE ALT OR VEL INFORMATION
022663,001548:                                                                                                  #                C) N SAMPLES OF RR DATA COULD NOT BE OBTAINED FROM 2N TRIES
022664,001549:                                                                                                  #                   WITH EITHER THE AL
022665,001550: 
022666,001551:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE:
022667,001552: 
022668,001553:                                                                                                  #        L       TC      SETTRKF
022669,001554:

022671,001556:

022714,001599:                                                                                                  #  Page 526
022715,001600:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME:  RRTURNON
022716,001601: 
022717,001602:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION:
022718,001603: 
022719,001604:                                                                                                  #        RRTURNON IS THE TURN-ON SEQUENCE WHICH, ALONG WTIH
022720,001605:                                                                                                  #        RRZEROSB, ZEROES THE CDU'S AND DETERMINES THE RR MODE.
022721,001606:                                                                                                  #        INITIALLY, CONTROL IS TRANSFERRED TO RRZEROSB FOR THE
022722,001607:                                                                                                  #        ACTUAL TURN-ON SEQUENCE.  UPON RETURN THE PROGRAM
022723,001608:                                                                                                  #        WAITS 1 SECOND BEFORE REMOVING THE TURN-ON FLAG
022724,001609:                                                                                                  #        (RADMODES BIT1) SO THE REPOSITION ROUTINE WON'T
022725,001610:                                                                                                  #        INITIATE PROGRAM ALARM 00501.  A CHECK IS THEN MADE
022726,001611:                                                                                                  #        TO SEE IF A PROGRAM IS USING THE RR (STATE BIT 7).  IF
022727,001612:                                                                                                  #        SO, THE PROGRAM EXITS TO ENDRADAR SO THAT THE RR CDU
022728,001613:                                                                                                  #        FAIL FLAG (RADMODES BIT 7) CAN BE CHECKED BEFORE
022729,001614:                                                                                                  #        RETURNING TO THE WAITING PROGRAM.  IF NOT, THE PROGRAM EXITS
022730,001615:                                                                                                  #        TO TASKOVER.
022731,001616: 
022732,001617:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE:  WAITLIST TASK FROM RRAUTCHK IF THE RR POWER-ON AUTO
022733,001618:                                                                                                  #  BIT (CHAN 33 BIT 2) CHANGES TO 0 AND NO PROGRAM WAS USING 
022734,001619:                                                                                                  #  THE RR (STATE BIT 7).
022735,001620: 
022736,001621:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED:
022737,001622: 
022738,001623:                                                                                                  #        RADMODES, STATE
022739,001624: 
022740,001625:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED:  RRZEROSB, FIXDELAY, TASKOVER, ENDRADAR
022741,001626: 
022742,001627:                                                                                                  #  JOBS OR TASKS INITIATED:
022743,001628:                                                                                                  #        
022744,001629:                                                                                                  #        NONE

022746,001631:                                                                                                  #  ALARMS:  NONE (SEE RRZEROSB)

022763,001648:                                                                                                  #  Page 527
022764,001649:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME:  RRZEROSB
022765,001650: 
022766,001651:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION:
022767,001652: 
022768,001653:                                                                                                  #        RRZEROSB IS A CLOSED SUBROUTINE TO ZERO THE RR CDU'S,
022769,001654:                                                                                                  #        DETERMINE THE RR MODE, AND TURN ON THE TRACKER FAIL
022770,001655:                                                                                                  #        LAMP IF REQUIRED.  INITIALLY THE RR CDU ZERO BIT (CHAN 12
022771,001656:                                                                                                  #        BIT 1) IS SET.  FOLLOWING A 20 MILLISECOND WAIT, THE LGC
022772,001657:                                                                                                  #        RR CDU COUNTERS (OPTY, OPTX) ARE SET = 0 AFTER 
022773,001658:                                                                                                  #        WHICH THE RR CDU ZERO DISCRETE (CHAN 12 BIT 1) IS
022774,001659:                                                                                                  #        REMOVED.  A 4 SECOND WAIT IS SET TO ALL THE RR CDU'S
022775,001660:                                                                                                  #        TO REPEAT THE ACTUAL TRUNNION AND SHAFT ANGLES.  THE
022776,001661:                                                                                                  #        RR CDU ZERO FLAG (RADMODES BIT 13) IS REMOVED.  THE
022777,001662:                                                                                                  #        CONTENTS OF OPTY IS THEN CHECKED TO SEE IF THE TRUNNION
022778,001663:                                                                                                  #        ANGLE IS LESS THAN 90 DEGREES.  IF NOT, BIT 12 OF
022779,001664:                                                                                                  #        RADMODES IS SET = 1 TO INDICATE RR ANTENNA MODE 2.
022780,001665:                                                                                                  #        IF LESS THAN 90 DEGREES, BIT 12 OF RADMODES IS SET = 0 TO
022781,001666:                                                                                                  #        INDICATE RR ANTENNA MODE 1.  SETTRKF IS THEN CALLED TO
022782,001667:                                                                                                  #        SEE IF THE TRACKER FAIL LAMP SHOULD BE TURNED ON.
022783,001668: 
022784,001669:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE:  L  TC  RRZEROSB  (FROM RRTURNON AND RRZERO)

022786,001671:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED:
022787,001672: 
022788,001673:                                                                                                  #        RADMODES (BIT 13 SET), DSPTAB +11D
022789,001674:

022840,001725:                                                                                                  #  Page 529
022841,001726:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME:  DORREPOS
022842,001727: 
022843,001728:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION:
022844,001729: 
022845,001730:                                                                                                  #        DORREPOS IS A SEQUENCE OF TASKS TO DRIVE THE RENDEZVOUS RADAR
022846,001731:                                                                                                  #        TO A SAFE POSITION.  INIITALLY SETRRECR IS CALLED WHERE THE RR
022847,001732:                                                                                                  #        ERROR COUNTERS (CHAN 12 BIT 2) ARE ENABLED AND LASTYCMD
022848,001733:                                                                                                  #        AND LASTXCMD SET = 0 TO INDICATE THE DIFFERENCE BETWEEN THE
022849,001734:                                                                                                  #        DESIRED STATE AND PRESENT STATE OF THE COMMANDS.  THE RR
022850,001735:                                                                                                  #        TURN-ON FLAG (RADMODES BIT 1) IS CHECKED AND IF NOT PRESENT,
022851,001736:                                                                                                  #        PROGRAM ALARM 00501 IS REQUESTED BEFORE CONTINUING.  IN EITHER
022852,001737:                                                                                                  #        CASE, FOLLOWING A 20 MILLISECOND WAIT THE PROGRAM CHECKS THE CURRENT
022853,001738:                                                                                                  #        RR ANTENNA MODE (RADMODES BIT 12).  RRTONLY IS THEN CALLED
022854,001739:                                                                                                  #        TO DRIVE THE TRUNNION ANGLE TO 0 DEGREES IF IN MODE 1 AND TO 180
022855,001740:                                                                                                  #        DEGREES IF IN MODE 2.  UPON RETURN, THE CURRENT RR ANTENNA
022856,001741:                                                                                                  #        MODE (RADMODES BIT 12) IS AGAIN CHECKED.  RRSONLY IS THEN
022857,001742:                                                                                                  #        CALLED TO DRIVE THE SHAFT ANGLE TO 0 DEGREES IF IN MODE 1 AND TO
022858,001743:                                                                                                  #        -90 DEGREES IF IN MODE 2.  IF DURING RRTONLY OR RRSONLY A
022859,001744:                                                                                                  #        REMODE HAS BEEN REQUESTED (RADMODES BIT 14), AND ALWAYS
022860,001745:                                                                                                  #        FOLLOWING COMPLETION OF RRSONLY, CONTROL IS TRANFERRED TO
022861,001746:                                                                                                  #        REPOSRPT.  HERE THE REPOSITION FLAG (RADMODES BIT 11) IS 
022862,001747:                                                                                                  #        REMOVED.  A CHECK IS THEN MADE ON THE DESIGNATE FLAG (RADMODES
022863,001748:                                                                                                  #        BIT 10).  IF PRESENT, CONTROL IS TRANSFERRED TO BEGDES.  IF NOT PRESENT
022864,001749:                                                                                                  #        INDICATING NO FURTHER ANTENNA CONTROL REQUIRED, THE RR ERROR
022865,001750:                                                                                                  #        COUNTER BIT (CHAN 12 BIT 2) IS REMOVED AND THE ROUTINE EXITS TO
022866,001751:                                                                                                  #        TASKOVER.
022867,001752: 
022868,001753:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE:
022869,001754: 
022870,001755:                                                                                                  #        WAITLIST CALL FROM RRGIMON IF TRUNNION AND SHAFT CDU ANGLES
022871,001756:                                                                                                  #        NOT WITHIN LIMITS OF CURRENT MODE.
022872,001757: 
022873,001758:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED:
022874,001759: 
022875,001760:                                                                                                  #        RADMODES
022876,001761: 
022877,001762:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED

022933,001818:                                                                                                  #  Page 531
022934,001819:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME:  REMODE
022935,001820: 
022936,001821:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION
022937,001822: 
022938,001823:                                                                                                  #        REMODE IS THE GENERAL REMODING SUBROUTINE.  IT DRIVES THE
022939,001824:                                                                                                  #        TRUNNION ANGLE TO 0 DEGREES IF THE CURRENT MODE IS MODE 1,
022940,001825:                                                                                                  #        180 DEGREES FOR MODE 2, THEN DRIVES THE SHAFT ANGLE TO -45
022941,001826:                                                                                                  #        DEGREES, AND FINALLY DRIVES THE TRUNNION ANGLE TO -130 DEGREES,
022942,001827:                                                                                                  #        TO PLACE THE RR IN MODE 2, -50 DEGREES FOR MODE 1, BEFORE
022943,001828:                                                                                                  #        INITIATING 2-AXIS CONTROL.  ALL REMODING IS DONE WITH SINGLE
022944,001829:                                                                                                  #        AXIS ROTATIONS (RR1AXIS).  INITIALLY THE RR ANTENNA MODE FLAG
022945,001830:                                                                                                  #        (RADMODES BIT 12) IS CHECKED.  CONTROL IS THEN TRANSFERRED TO
022946,001831:                                                                                                  #        RRTONLY TO DRIVE THR TRUNNION ANGLE TO 0 DEGREES IF IN MODE 1
022947,001832:                                                                                                  #        OR 180 DEGREES IF IN MODE 2.  RRSONLY IS THEN CALLED TO DRIVE
022948,001833:                                                                                                  #        THE SHAFT ANGLE TO -45 DEGREES. THE RR ANTENNA MODE FLAG
022949,001834:                                                                                                  #        (RADMODES BIT 12) IS CHECKED AGAIN.  CONTROL IS AGAIN
022950,001835:                                                                                                  #        TRANSFERRED TO RRTONLY TO DRIVE THE TRUNNION ANGLE TO -130
022951,001836:                                                                                                  #        DEGREES TO PLACE THE RR IN MODE 2 IF CURRENTLY IN MODE 1 OR TO
022952,001837:                                                                                                  #        -50 DEGREES IF IN MODE 2 TO PLACE THE RR IN MODE 1.  RMODINV
022953,001838:                                                                                                  #        IS THEN CALLED TO SET RADMODES BIT 12 TO INDICATE THE NEW
022954,001839:                                                                                                  #        RR ANTENNA MODE.  THE REMODE FLAG (RADMODES BIT 14)
022955,001840:                                                                                                  #        IS REMOVED TO INDICATE THAT REMODING IS COMPLETE.  THE PROGRAM
022956,001841:                                                                                                  #        THEN EXITS TO STDESIG TO BEGIN 2-AXIS CONTROL.
022957,001842: 
022958,001843:                                                                                                  #  CALLIN SEQUENCE:
022959,001844: 
022960,001845:                                                                                                  #        FROM BEGDES WHEN REMODE FLAG (RADMODES BIT 14) IS SET.
022961,001846:                                                                                                  #        THIS FLAG MAY BE SET IN RRDESSM AND RRDESNB IF RRLIMCHK
022962,001847:                                                                                                  #        DETERMINES THAT THE DESIRED ANGLES ARE WITHIN THE LIMITS OF THE
022963,001848:                                                                                                  #        OTHER MODE.
022964,001849: 
022965,001850:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INIITIALIZATION REQUIRED:
022966,001851: 
022967,001852:                                                                                                  #        RADMODES
022968,001853: 
022969,001854:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED:
022970,001855:

022972,001857:

022974,001859:

023031,001916:                                                                                                  #  Page 533
023032,001917:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAMES:        RRTONLY, RRSONLY
023033,001918: 
023034,001919:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION:
023035,001920: 
023036,001921:                                                                                                  #        RRTONLY AND RRSONLY ARE SUBROUTINES FOR DOING SINGLE AXIS
023037,001922:                                                                                                  #        RR MANEUVERS FOR REMODE AND REPOSITION.  IT DRIVES TO
023038,001923:                                                                                                  #        WITHIN 1 DEGREE.  INITIALLY, AT RR1AX2, THE REMODE AND REPOSITION
023039,001924:                                                                                                  #        FLAGS (RADMODES BITS 14, 11) ARE CHECKED.  IF BOTH EXIST,
023040,001925:                                                                                                  #        THE PROGRAM EXITS TO REPOSRPT (SEE DORREPOS).  THIS INDICATES
023041,001926:                                                                                                  #        THAT SOMEONE POSSIBLY REQUESTED A DESIGNATE (RADMODES BIT 10)
023042,001927:                                                                                                  #        WHICH REQUIRES A REMODE (RADMODES BIT 14) AND THAT A
023043,001928:                                                                                                  #        REPOSITION IS IN PROGRESS (RADMODES BIT 11).  IF NONE
023044,001929:                                                                                                  #        OR ONLY ONE OF THE FLAGS EXIST, REMODE OR REPOSITION, MAGSUB
023045,001930:                                                                                                  #        IS CALLED TO SEE IF THE APPROPRIATE ANGLE IS WITHIN 1 DEGREE.  IF YES,
023046,001931:                                                                                                  #        CONTROL RETURNS TO THE CALLING ROUTINE.  IF NOT, CONTROL IS
023047,001932:                                                                                                  #        TRANSFERRED TO RROUT FOR SINGLE AXIS MANEUVERS WITH THE OTHER
023048,001933:                                                                                                  #        ANGLE SET = 0.  FOLLOWING A .5 SECOND WAIT, THE ABOVE PROCEDURE IS
023049,001934:                                                                                                  #        REPEATED.
023050,001935: 
023051,001936:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE:     L-1     CAF     *ANGLE*         (DESIRED ANGLE SCALED PI)
023052,001937:                                                                                                  #                        L       TC      RRTONLY         (TRUNNION ONLY)
023053,001938:                                                                                                  #                        RRSONLY                         (SHAFT ONLY)
023054,001939:                                                                                                  #                        RRTONLY IS CALLED BY PREPOS29;
023055,001940:                                                                                                  #                        RRTONLY AND RRSONLY ARE CALLED BY DORREPOS AND REMODE
023056,001941: 
023057,001942:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED:
023058,001943: 
023059,001944:                                                                                                  #        C(A) = DESIRED ANGLE, RADMODES
023060,001945: 
023061,001946:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED:
023062,001947: 
023063,001948:                                                                                                  #        FIXDELAY, REPOSRPT, MAGSUB, RROUT
023064,001949:

023066,001951: 
023067,001952:                                                                                                  #        NONE
023068,001953:

023070,001955:

023072,001957:                                                                                                  #        BITS 14, 11)

023125,002010:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME:  RROUT
023126,002011: 
023127,002012:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION:
023128,002013: 
023129,002014:                                                                                                  #        RROUT RECEIVES RR GYRO COMMANDS IN TANG, TANG +1 IN RR
023130,002015:                                                                                                  #        ERROR COUNTER SCALING.  RROUT THEN LIMITS THEM AND
023131,002016:                                                                                                  #        GENERATES COMMANDS TO THE CDU TO ADJUST THE ERROR COUNTERS
023132,002017:                                                                                                  #        TO THE DESIRED VALUES.  INITIALLY MAGSUB CHECKS THE MAGNITUDE OF
023133,002018:                                                                                                  #        THE COMMAND (SHAFT ON 1ST PASS) TO SEE IF IT IS GREATER THAN
023134,002019:                                                                                                  #        384 PULSES.  IF NOT, CONTROL IS TRANFERRED TO RROUTLIM TO
023135,002020:                                                                                                  #        LIMIT THE COMMAND TO +384 OR -384 PULSES.  THE DIFFERENCE IS
023136,002021:                                                                                                  #        THEN CALCULATED BETWEEN THE DESIRED STATE AND TEH PRESENT STATE OF
023137,002022:                                                                                                  #        THE ERROR COUNTER AS RECORDED IN LASTYCMD AND LASTXCMD.
023138,002023:                                                                                                  #        THE RESULT IS STORED IN OPTXCMD (1ST PASS) AND OPTYCMD (2ND
023139,002024:                                                                                                  #        PASS).  FOLLOWING THE SECOND PASS, FOR THE TRUNNION COMMAND, THE
023140,002025:                                                                                                  #        OCDUT AND OCDUS ERROR COUNTER DRIVE BITS (CHAN 14 BITS 12, 11)
023141,002026:                                                                                                  #        ARE SET.  THIS PROGRAM THEN EXITS TO THE CALLING PROGRAM.
023142,002027: 
023143,002028:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE:
023144,002029:                                                                                                  #        
023145,002030:                                                                                                  #        L TC RROUT (WITH RUPT INHIBITED) RROUT IS CALLED BY
023146,002031:                                                                                                  #        RRTONLY, RRSONLY, AND DODES
023147,002032: 
023148,002033:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQURIED:
023149,002034: 
023150,002035:                                                                                                  #        TANG, TANG +1 (DESIRED COMMANDS), LASTYCMD, LASTXCMD
023151,002036:                                                                                                  #        (1ST PASS = 0), RR ERROR COUNTER ENAGLE SET (CHAN 12 BIT 2).
023152,002037: 
023153,002038:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED:
023154,002039:

023233,002118: 
023234,002119:                                                                                                  #  Page 538
023235,002120:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME:  RRDESSM
023236,002121: 
023237,002122:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION:
023238,002123: 
023239,002124:                                                                                                  #        THIS INTERPRETIVE ROUTINE WILL DESIGNATE, IF DESIRED ANGLES ARE
023240,002125:                                                                                                  #        WITHIN THE LIMITS OF EITHER MODE, TO A LINE-OF-SIGHT (LOS) VECTOR
023241,002126:                                                                                                  #        (HALF-UNIT) KNOWN WITH RESPECT TO THE STABLE MEMBER PRESENT
023242,002127:                                                                                                  #        ORIENTATION.  INITIALLY THE IMU CDU'S ARE READ AND CONTROL
023243,002128:                                                                                                  #        TRANSFERRED TO SMNB TO TRANSFORM THE LOS VECTOR FROM STABLE
023244,002129:                                                                                                  #        MEMBER TO NAVIGATION BASE COORDINATES (SEE STG MEMO 699)
023245,002130:                                                                                                  #        RRANGLES IS THEN CALLED TO CALCULATE THE RR GIMBAL ANGLES,
023246,002131:                                                                                                  #        TRUNNION AND SHAFT, FOR BOT THE PRESENT AND ALTERNATE MODE.
023247,002132:                                                                                                  #        RRLIMCHK IS CALLED TO SEE IF THE ANGLES CALCULATED FOR THE
023248,002133:                                                                                                  #        PRESENT MODE ARE WITHIN LIMITS.  IF WITHIN LIMITS, THE RETUREN
023249,002134:                                                                                                  #        LOCATION IS INCREMENTED, INASMUCH AS NO VEHICLE MANEUVER IS
023250,002135:                                                                                                  #        REQUIRED, BEFORE EXITING TO STARTDES.  IF NOT WITHIN THE LIMITS OF THE
023251,002136:                                                                                                  #        CURRENT MODE, TRYSWS IS CALLED.  FOLLOWING INVERTING OF THE RR
023252,002137:                                                                                                  #        ANTENNA MODE FLAG (RADMODES BIT 12), RRLIMCHK IS CALLED
023253,002138:                                                                                                  #        TO SEE IF THE ANGLES CALCULATED FOR THE ALTERNATE MODE ARE WITHIN
023254,002139:                                                                                                  #        LIMITS.  IF YES, THE RR ANTENNA MODE FLAG IS AGAIN INVERTED,
023255,002140:                                                                                                  #        THE REMODE FLAG (RADMODES BIT 14) SET, AND THE RETURN LOCATION
023256,002141:                                                                                                  #        INCREMENTED, TO INDICATE NO VEHICLE MANEUVER IS REQUIRED, BEFORE
023257,002142:                                                                                                  #        EXITING TO STARTDES.  IF THESE ANGLES ARE NOT WITHIN LIMITS
023258,002143:                                                                                                  #        OF THE ALTERNATE MODE, THE RR ANTENNA MODE FLAG (RADMODES
023259,002144:                                                                                                  #        BIT 12) IS INVERTED BEFORE RETURNING DIRECTLY TO THE CALLING PROGRAM
023260,002145:                                                                                                  #        TO INDICATE THAT A VEHICLE MANEUVER IS REQUIRED.
023261,002146: 
023262,002147:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE:
023263,002148: 
023264,002149:                                                                                                  #        L       STCALL  RRTARGET        (LOS HALF-UNIT VECTOR IN SM COORDINATES)
023265,002150:                                                                                                  #        L+1     RRDESM
023266,002151:                                                                                                  #        L+2     BASIC                   (VEHICLE MANEUVER REQUIRED)
023267,002152:                                                                                                  #        L+3     BASIC                   (NO VEHICLE MANEUVER REQUIRED)
023268,002153: 
023269,002154:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED:
023270,002155: 
023271,002156:                                                                                                  #        RRTARGET, RADMODES
023272,002157: 
023273,002158:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED:
023274,002159: 
023275,002160:                                                                                                  #        READCDUS, SMNB, RRANGLES, RRLIMCHK, TRYSWS (ACTUALLY
023276,002161:                                                                                                  #        PART OF), RMODINV
023277,002162: 
023278,002163:                                                                                                  #  JOBS OR TASKS INITIATED:
023279,002164: 
023280,002165:                                                                                                  #        NONE
023281,002166: 
023282,002167:                                                                                                  #  ALARMS:  NONE
023283,002168: 
023284,002169:                                                                                                  #  EXIT:  L+2 (NEITHER SET OF ANGLES ARE WITHIN LIMITS OF RELATED MODE)
023285,002170:                                                                                                  #  STARTDES (DESIGNATE POSSIBLE AT PRESENT VEHICLES ATTITUDE -- RETURNS
023286,002171:                                                                                                  #  TO L+3 FROM STARTDES)
023287,002172:

023293,002178: 25,2377           47537                                    CDUTRIG

023299,002184: 25,2404           26133                                    RRANGLES                              #  ALTERNATE MODE.

023324,002209:                                                                                                  #  Page 540
023325,002210:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME:  STARTDES
023326,002211: 
023327,002212:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION:
023328,002213: 
023329,002214:                                                                                                  #        STARTDES IS ENTERED WHEN WE ARE READY TO BEGIN DESIGNATION.
023330,002215:                                                                                                  #        BIT 14 OF RADMODES IS ALREADY SET IF A REMODE IS REQUIRED.
023331,002216:                                                                                                  #        AT THIS TIME, THE RR ANTENNA MAY BE IN A REPOSITON
023332,002217:                                                                                                  #        OPERATION.  IN THIS CASE, IF A REMODE IS REQUIRED IT MAY HAVE
023333,002218:                                                                                                  #        ALREADY BEGUN BUT IN ANY CASE THE REPOSITION WILL BE INTERRUPTED.
023334,002219:                                                                                                  #        OTHERWISE, THE REPOSITION WILL BE COMPLETED BEFORE 2-AXIS
023335,002220:                                                                                                  #        DESIGNATION BEGINS.  INITIALLY DESCOUNT IS SET = 60 TO INDICATE
023336,002221:                                                                                                  #        THAT 30 SECONDS WILL BE ALLOWED FOR THE RR DATA GOOD INBIT
023337,002222:                                                                                                  #        (CHAN 33 BIT 4) IF LOCK-ON IS DESIRED (STATE BIT 5).  BIT 10
023338,002223:                                                                                                  #        OF RADMODES IS SET TO SHOW THAT A DESIGNATE IS REQUIRED.
023339,002224:                                                                                                  #        THE REPOSITON FLAG (RADMODES BIT 11) IS CHECKED.  IF SET,
023340,002225:                                                                                                  #        THE PROGRAM EXITS TO L+3 OF THE CALLING PROGRAM (SEE RRDESSM
023341,002226:                                                                                                  #        AND RRDESNB).  THE PROGRAM WILL BEGIN DESIGNATING TO THE DESIRED
023342,002227:                                                                                                  #        ANGLES FOLLOWING THE REPOSITON OR REMODE IF ONE WAS
023343,002228:                                                                                                  #        REQUESTED.  IF THE REPOSITON FLAG IS NOT SET, SETRRECR IS CALLED
023344,002229:                                                                                                  #        WITH SETS THE RR ERROR COUNTER ENABLE BIT (CHAN 12 BIT 2)
023345,002230:                                                                                                  #        AND SETS LASTYCMD AND LASTXCMD = 0 TO INDICATE THE
023346,002231:                                                                                                  #        DIFFERENCE BETWEEN THE PRESENT AND DESIRED STATE OF THE ERROR
023347,002232:                                                                                                  #        COUNTERS.  A 20 MILLISECOND WAITLIST CALL IS SET FOR BEGDES
023348,002233:                                                                                                  #        AFTER WHICH THE PROGRAM EXITS TO L+3 OF TEH CALLING PROGRAM.
023349,002234: 
023350,002235:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE:
023351,002236: 
023352,002237:                                                                                                  #        FROM RRDESSM AND RRDESNB WHEN ANGLES WITHIN LIMITS.
023353,002238: 
023354,002239:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED:
023355,002240: 
023356,002241:                                                                                                  #        RADMODES, (SEE DODES)
023357,002242:

023359,002244:
