023498,002383:                                                                                                  #  Page 545
023499,002384:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME:  BEGDES
023500,002385: 
023501,002386:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION:
023502,002387: 
023503,002388:                                                                                                  #        BEGDES CHECKS VARIOUS DESIGNATE REQUESTS AND REQUESTS THE
023504,002389:                                                                                                  #        ACTUAL RR DESIGNATION.  INITIALLY A CHECK IS MADE TO SEE IF A
023505,002390:                                                                                                  #        REMODE (RADMODES BIT 14) IS REQUESTED OR IN PROGRESS.  IF SO,
023506,002391:                                                                                                  #        CONTROL IS TRANFERRED TO STDESIG AFTER ROUTINE REMODE IS
023507,002392:                                                                                                  #        EXECUTED.  IF NO REMODE, STDESIG IS IMMEDIATELY CALLED WHERE
023508,002393:                                                                                                  #        FIRST THE REPOSITION FLAG (RADMODES BIT 11) IS CHECKED.  IF
023509,002394:                                                                                                  #        PRESENT, THE DESIGNATE FLAG (RADMODES BIT 10) IS REMOVED
023510,002395:                                                                                                  #        AFTER WHICH THE PROGRAM EXITS TO RDBADEND.  IF THE REPOSITION
023511,002396:                                                                                                  #        FLAG IS NOT PRESET, THE CONTINUOUS DESIGNATE FLAG (RADMODES
023512,002397:                                                                                                  #        BIT 15) IS CHECKED.  IF PRESENT, AN EXECUTIVE CALL IS IMMEDIATELY
023513,002398:                                                                                                  #        MADE FOR DODES AFTER WHICH A .5 SECOND WAIT IS INITIATED BEFORE
023514,002399:                                                                                                  #        REPEATING AT STDESIG.  IF THE RR SEARCH ROUTINE (LRS24.1) IS DESIGNATING
023515,002400:                                                                                                  #        TO A NEW POINT (NEWPTFLG SET) THE CURRENT DESIGNATE TASK IS TERMINATED.
023516,002401:                                                                                                  #        IF CONTINUOUS DESIGNATE IS NOT WANTED, THE DESIGNATE FLAG (RADMODES
023517,002402:                                                                                                  #        BIT 10) IS CHECKED.  IF NOT PRESENT, THE PROGRAM EXITS TO ENDRADAR TO
023518,002403:                                                                                                  #        CHECK RR CDU FAIL BEFORE RETURNING TO THE CALLING PROGRAM.  IF DESIGNATE
023519,002404:                                                                                                  #        IS STILL REQUIRED, DESCOUNT IS CHECKED TO SEE IF THE 30 SECONDS HAS
023520,002405:                                                                                                  #        EXPIRED BEFORE RECEIVING THE RR DATA GOOD (CHAN 33 BIT 4)
023521,002406:                                                                                                  #        SIGNAL.  IF OUT OF TIME, PROGRAM ALARM 00503 IS REQUESTED, THE
023522,002407:                                                                                                  #        RR AUTO TRACKER ENABLE AND RR ERROR COUNTER ENABLE
023523,002408:                                                                                                  #        (CHAN 12 BITS 14,2) BITS REMOVED, AND THE DESIGNATE FLAG
023524,002409:                                                                                                  #        (RADMODES BIT 10) REMOVED BEFORE EEXITING TO RDBADEND.  IF
023525,002410:                                                                                                  #        TIME HAS NOT EXPIRED, DESCOUNT IS DECREMENTED, THE
023526,002411:                                                                                                  #        EXECUTIVE CALL MADE FOR DODES, AND A .5 SECOND WAIT INITIATED
023527,002412:                                                                                                  #        BEFORE REPEATING THIS PROCEDURE AT STDESIG.
023528,002413: 
023529,002414:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE:
023530,002415: 
023531,002416:                                                                                                  #        WAITLIST CALL FROM STARTDES
023532,002417:                                                                                                  #        TCF BEGDES FROM DORREPOS
023533,002418:                                                                                                  #        TC STDESIG RETURNING, FROM REMODE
023534,002419: 
023535,002420:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED:
023536,002421: 
023537,002422:                                                                                                  #        DESCOUNT, FINDVAC
023538,002423: 
023539,002424:                                                                                                  #  JOBS OR TASKS INITIATED:  DODES
023540,002425: 
023541,002426:                                                                                                  #  ALARMS:  PROGRAM ALARM 00503 (30 SECONDS HAVE EXPIRED) WITH NO RR DATA
023542,002427:                                                                                                  #  GOOD (CHAN 33 BIT 4) RECEIVED WHEN LOCK-ON (STATE BIT 5) WAS REQUESTED.
023543,002428: 
023544,002429:                                                                                                  #  EXIT:         TASKOVER (SEARCH PATTERN DESIGNATING TO NEW POINT)
023545,002430:                                                                                                  #                ENDRADAR (NO DESIGNATE -- RADMODES BIT 10)
023546,002431:                                                                                                  #                RDBADEND (REPOSITION OR 30 SECONDS EXPIRED)
023547,002432:

023553,002438: 25,2577           02171                           TC       REMODE                                
023554,002439: 25,2600           05221        DESLOOP            TC       FIXDELAY                              #  2 SAMPLES PER SECOND.
023555,002440: 25,2601           00062                           DEC      50         B-14

023560,002445: 25,2605           12623                           TCF      BADDES                                #  REPOSITION TO BE IN PROGRESS.

023585,002470: 25,2631           05105                           TC       FINDVAC                               
023586,002471: 25,2632  E7,1456                                  EBANK=   LOSCOUNT                              
023587,002472: 25,2632           02636 52067                     2CADR    DODES                                 
023588,002473: 
023589,002474: 25,2634           12600                           TCF      DESLOOP                               
023590,002475: 
023591,002476: 25,2635           20002        B14+B2             OCT      20002                                 
023592,002477: 
023593,002478:                                                                                                  #  Page 547
023594,002479:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME:  DODES
023595,002480: 
023596,002481:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION:
023597,002482: 
023598,002483:                                                                                                  #        DODES CALCULATES AND REQUESTS ISSUANCE OF RR GYRO TORQUE
023599,002484:                                                                                                  #        COMMANDS.  INITIALLY THE CURRENT RR CDU ANGLES ARE STORED AND
023600,002485:                                                                                                  #        THE LOS HALF-UNIT VECTOR TRANSFORMED FROM STABLE MEMBER TO
023601,002486:                                                                                                  #        NAVIGATION BASE COORDINATES VIA SMNB IF NECESSARY.  THE
023602,002487:                                                                                                  #        SHAFT AND TRUNNION COMMANDS ARE THEN CALCULATED AS FOLLOWS:
023603,002488:                                                                                                  #                + SHAFT = LOS . (COS(S), 0, -SIN(S))  (DOT PRODUCT)
023604,002489:                                                                                                  #                - TRUNNION = LOS . (SIN(T)SIN(S), COS(T), SIN(T)COS(S))
023605,002490:                                                                                                  #        THE SIGN OF THE SHAFT COMMAND IS THEN REVERSED IF IN MODE 2
023606,002491:                                                                                                  #        (RADMODES BIT 12) BECAUSE A RELAY IN THE RR REVERSES THE 
023607,002492:                                                                                                  #        POLARITY OF THE COMMAND.  AT RRSCALUP EACH COMMAND IS
023608,002493:                                                                                                  #        SCALED AND IF EITHER, OR BOTH, OF THE COMMANDS IS GREATER THAN
023609,002494:                                                                                                  #        .5 DEGREES, MPAC +1 IS SET POSITIVE.  IF A CONTINUOUS DESIGNATE 
023610,002495:                                                                                                  #        (RADMODES BIT 15) IS DESIRED AND THE SEARCH ROUTINE IS NOT OPERATING,
023611,002496:                                                                                                  #        THE RR AUTO TRACKER ENABLE BIT (CHAN 12 BIT 14) IS CLEARED AND RROUT
023612,002497:                                                                                                  #        CALLED TO PUT OUT THE COMMANDS PROVIDED NO REPOSITION (RADMODES BIT 11)
023613,002498:                                                                                                  #        IS IN PROGRESS.  IF A CONTINUOUS DESIGNATE AND THE SEARCH ROUTINE IS
023614,002499:                                                                                                  #        OPERATING (SRCHOPT FLAT SET) THE TRACK ENABLE IS NOT CLEARED.  IF NO
023615,002500:                                                                                                  #        CONTINUOUS DESIGNATE AND BOTH COMMANDS ARE NOT LESS THAN .5 DEGREES AS
023616,002501:                                                                                                  #        INDICATED BY MPAC +1, THE RR AUTO TRACKER ENABLE BIT (CHAN 12 BIT 14) IS
023617,002502:                                                                                                  #        CLEARED AND RROUT CALLED TO PUT OUT THE COMMANDS PROVIDED NO REPOSITON
023618,002503:                                                                                                  #        (RADMODES BIT 11) IS IN PROGRESS.  IF BOTH COMMANDS ARE LESS THAN .5
023619,002504:                                                                                                  #        DEGREES AS INDICATED BY MPAC+1, THE RR AUTO TRACKER ENABLE BIT
023620,002505:                                                                                                  #        (CHAN 12 BIT 14) IS CLEARED AND RROUT CALLED TO PUT OUT THE
023621,002506:                                                                                                  #        COMMANDS PROVIDED NO REPOSITION (RADMODES BIT 11) IS IN
023622,002507:                                                                                                  #        PROGRESS.  IF BOTH COMMANDS ARE LESS THAN .5 DEGREES, THE
023623,002508:                                                                                                  #        LOCK-ON FLAG (STATE BIT 5) IS CHECKED.  IF NOT PRESETN, THE
023624,002509:                                                                                                  #        DESIGNATE FLAG (RADMODES BIT 10) IS CLEARED, AND ENDOFJOB
023625,002510:                                                                                                  #        CALLED.  IF LOCK-ON IS DESIRED, THE RR AUTO TRACKER (CHAN 12
023626,002511:                                                                                                  #        BIT 14) IS ENABLED FOLLOWED BY A CHECK OF THE RECEIPT OF THE
023627,002512:                                                                                                  #        RR DATA GOOD (CHAN 33 BIT 4) SIGNAL.  IF RR DATA GOOD
023628,002513:                                                                                                  #        PRESENT, THE DESIGNATE FLAG (RADMODES BIT 10) IS CLEARED,
023629,002514:                                                                                                  #        THE RR ERROR COUNTER ENABLE BIT (CHAN 12 BIT 2) IS CLEARED,
023630,002515:                                                                                                  #        AND ENDOFJOB CALLED.  IF RR DATA GOOD IS NOT PRESENT, RROUT
023631,002516:                                                                                                  #        IS CALLED TO PUT OUT THE COMMANDS PROVIDED NO REPOSITION
023632,002517:                                                                                                  #        (RADMODES BIT 11) IS IN PROGRESS AFTER WHICH THE JOB IS TERMINATED
023633,002518:                                                                                                  #        VIA ENDOFJOB.
023634,002519: 
023635,002520:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE:
023636,002521: 
023637,002522:                                                                                                  #        EXECUTIVE CALL EVERY .5 SECONDS FROM BEGDES.
023638,002523: 
023639,002524:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED:
023640,002525: 
023641,002526:                                                                                                  #        RRTARGET (HALF-UNIT LOS VECTOR IN EITHER SM OR NB COORDINATES),
023642,002527:                                                                                                  #        LOKONSW (STATE BIT 5), RRNBSW (STATE BIT 6), RADMODES
023643,002528: 
023644,002529:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED:
023645,002530: 
023646,002531:                                                                                                  #        READCDUS, SMNB, CDULOGIC, MAGSUB, RROUT
023647,002532:                                                                                                  #  Page 548
023648,002533: 
023649,002534:                                                                                                  #  JOBS OR TASKS INITIATED:
023650,002535: 
023651,002536:                                                                                                  #        NONE
023652,002537: 
023653,002538:                                                                                                  #  ALARMS:  NONE
023654,002539: 
023655,002540:                                                                                                  #  EXIT:  ENDOFJOB (ALWAYS)
023656,002541: 
023657,002542: 25,2636           00006        DODES              EXTEND                                         
023658,002543: 25,2637           30036                           DCA      CDUT                                  
023659,002544: 25,2640           53110                           DXCH     TANG

023661,002546: 25,2641           06037                           TC       INTPRET

023712,002597:                                                                                                  #  COMMANDED RATE AND ENABLE THE TRACKER IF WE ARE WITHIN .5 DEGREES OF THE TARGET.

024262,003147:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME:  LPS20.1 VECTOR EXTRAPOLATION AND LOS COMPUTATION
024263,003148:                                                                                                  #  MOD. NO. 2    BY J.D. COYNE   SDC     DATE 12-7-66
024264,003149: 
024265,003150:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRPIPTION:
024266,003151:                                                                                                  #        1)      EXTRAPOLATE THE LEM AND CSM VECTORS IN ACCORDANCE WITH THE TIME REFERRED TO IN CALLER + 1.
024267,003152:                                                                                                  #        2)      COMPUTES THE LOS VECTOR TO THE CSM, CONVERTS IT TO STABLE MEMBER COORDINATES AND STORES IT IN RRTARGET.
024268,003153:                                                                                                  #        3)      COMPUTES THE MAGNITUDE OF TEH LOS VECTOR AND STORES IT IN MLOSV
024269,003154: 
024270,003155:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE:     CALL
024271,003156:                                                                                                  #                                LPS20.1

024391,003276:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME:  LRS22.1 (DATA READ SUBROUTINE 1)
024392,003277:                                                                                                  #  MOD. NO.: 1           BY: P. VOLANTE  SDC             DATE:  11-15-66
024393,003278: 
024394,003279:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION:
024395,003280:                                                                                                  #        1)      READS RENDEZVOUS RADAR RANGE AND RANGE-RATE, TRUNNION AND SHAFT ANGLES, THREE CDU VALUES AND TIME.  CONVERTS THIS
024396,003281:                                                                                                  #                DATA AND LEAVES IT FOR THE MEASUREMENT INCORPORATION ROUTINE (LSR22.3).  CHECKS FOR THE RR DATA GOOD DISCRETE, FOR
024397,003282:                                                                                                  #                RR REPOSITION AND RR CDU FAIL
024398,003283:                                                                                                  #        2)      COMPARES RADAR LOS WITH LOS COMPUTED FROM STATE VECTORS TO SEE IF THEY ARE WITHIN THREE DEGREES
024399,003284:

024401,003286: 
024402,003287:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED:
024403,003288:                                                                                                  #        RRDOT           LPS20.1
024404,003289:                                                                                                  #        RRRANGE         BANKCALL
024405,003290:                                                                                                  #        RADSTALL        CDULOGIC
024406,003291:                                                                                                  #        RRNB            SMNB
024407,003292: 
024408,003293:                                                                                                  #  NORMAL EXIT:  RETURN TO CALLER+1 WITH MPAC SET TO +0
024409,003294: 
024410,003295:                                                                                                  #  ERROR EXITS:  RETURN TO CALLER+1 WITH ERROR CODE STORED IN MPAC AS FOLLOWS:
024411,003296:                                                                                                  #        00001 -- ERROR EXIT 1 -- RR DATA NO GOOD (NO RR DATA GOOD DISCRETE OR RR CDU FAIL OR RR REPOSITION)
024412,003297:                                                                                                  #        00002 -- ERROR EXIT 2 -- RR LOS NOT WITHIN THREE DEGREES OF LOS COMPUTED FROM STATE VECTORS
024413,003298: 
024414,003299:                                                                                                  #  ALARMS:  521 -- COULD NOT READ RADAR DATA (RR DATA GOOD DISCRETE NOT PRESENT BEFORE AND AFTER READING THE RADAR)
024415,003300:                                                                                                  #        (THIS ALARM IS ISSUED BY RADARREAD SUBROUTINE WHICH IS ENTERED FROM A RADARUPT)
024416,003301: 
024417,003302:                                                                                                  #  OUTPUT:  RRLOSVEC -- THE RR LINE-OF-SIGHT VECTOR (USED BY LRS22.2) -- A HALF-UNIT VECTOR
024418,003303:                                                                                                  #        RM -- THE RR RANGE READING (TO THE CSM) DP, IN METERS SCALED BY B-29 (USED BY LRS22.2 AND LRS22.3)
024419,003304: 
024420,003305:                                                                                                  #        ALL OF THE FOLLOWING OUTPUTS ARE USED BY LRS22.3:
024421,003306:                                                                                                  #                RDOTM -- THE RR RANGE-RATE READING, DP, IN METERS PER CENTISECOND, SCALED BY B-7
024422,003307:                                                                                                  #                RRTRUN -- THE RR TRUNNION ANGLE, DP, IN REVOLUTIONS, SCALED B0
024423,003308:                                                                                                  #                RRSHAFT -- RR SHAFT ANGLE, DP, IN REVOLUTIONS, SCALED B0
024424,003309:                                                                                                  #                AIG,AMG,AOG -- THE CDU ANGLES, THREE SP WORDS

024564,003449:                                                                                                  #  MOD. NO.: 1           BY: P. VOLANTE  SDC             DATE: 4-11-67
024565,003450: 
024566,003451:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION:
024567,003452:                                                                                                  #        (Yes, I know point #1 is missing.  It is missing from the program listing -- RSB 2003)
024568,003453:                                                                                                  #        2)  CHECKS IF THE RR LOS (I.E., THE RADAR BORESIGHT VECTOR) IS WITHIN 30 DEGREES OF THE LM +Z AXIS
024569,003454: 
024570,003455:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE:  BANKCALL FOR LRS22.2
024571,003456: 
024572,003457:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED:  G+N, AUTO, SETMAXDB
024573,003458: 
024574,003459:                                                                                                  #  NORMAL EXIT:  RETURN TO CALLER WITH MPAC SET TO +0 (VIA SWRETURN)
024575,003460: 
024576,003461:                                                                                                  #  ERROR EXIT:  RETURN TO CALLER WITH MPAC SET TO 00001 -- RADAR LOS NOT WITHIN 30 DEGREES OF LM +Z AXIS.
024577,003462: 
024578,003463:                                                                                                  #  ALARMS:  NONE
024579,003464: 
024580,003465:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED:
024581,003466:                                                                                                  #        RRLOSVEC -- THE RR LINE-OF-SIGHT VECTOR -- A HALF UNIT VECTOR COMPUTED BY LRS22.1
024582,003467:                                                                                                  #        RM -- RR RANGE, METERS B-29, FROM LRS22.1
024583,003468:                                                                                                  #        BIT 14 CHANNEL 31 -- INDICATES AUTOPILOT IS IN AUTO MODE
024584,003469:

024613,003498: 
024614,003499:                                                                                                  #  Page 574
024615,003500:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME -- LSR22.3                               DATE -- 29 MAY 1967
024616,003501:                                                                                                  #  MOD. NO 3                                             LOG SECTION -- P20-P25
024617,003502:                                                                                                  #  MOD. BY -- DANFORTH                                   ASSEMBLY LEMP20S REV 10
024618,003503: 
024619,003504:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION:
024620,003505:                                                                                                  #        THIS ROUTINE COMPUTES THE B-VECTORS ADN DELTA Q FOR EACH OF THE QUANTITIES MEASURED BY THE RENDEZVOUS
024621,003506:                                                                                                  #        RADAR.  (RANGE, RANGE RATE, SHAFT AND TRUNNION ANGLES).  THE ROUTINE CALLS THE INCORP1 AND INCORP2 ROUTINES
024622,003507:                                                                                                  #        WHICH COMPUTE THE DEVIATIONS AND CORRECT THE STATE VECTOR.
024623,003508: 
024624,003509:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE:
024625,003510:                                                                                                  #        THIS ROUTINE IS PART OF P20 RENDEZVOUS NAVIGATION FOR THE LM COMPUTER ONLY.  THE ROUTINE IS ENTERED FROM
024626,003511:                                                                                                  #        R22 LEM ONLY AND RETURNS DIRECTLY TO R22LEM FOLLOWING SUCCESSFUL INCORPORATION OF MEASURED DATA.  IF THE
024627,003512:                                                                                                  #        COMPUTED STATE VECTOR DEVATIONS EXCEED THE MAXIMUM PERMITTED.  THE ROUTINE RETURNS TO R22LEM TO DISPLAY
024628,003513:                                                                                                  #        THE DEVIATIONS.  IF THE ASTRONAUT ACCEPTS THE DATA R22LEM RETURNS TO LSR22.3 TO INCORPORATE THE
024629,003514:                                                                                                  #        DEVIATIONS INTO THE STATE VECTOR.  IF THE ASTRONAUT REJECTS THE DEVIATIONS, NO MORE MEASUREMENTS ARE
024630,003515:                                                                                                  #        PROCESSED FOR THIS MARK, I.E.,  R22LEM GETS THE NEXT MARK.
024631,003516: 
024632,003517:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED:
024633,003518:                                                                                                  #        WLINIT          LGCUPDTE        INTEGRV         INCORP1         ARCTAN
024634,003519:                                                                                                  #        GETULC          RADARANG        INCORP2         NBSM            INTSTALL
024635,003520: 
024636,003521:                                                                                                  #  OUTPUT:
024637,003522:                                                                                                  #        CORRECTED LM OR CSM STATE VECTOR (PERMANENT)
024638,003523:                                                                                                  #        NUMBER OF MARKS INCORPORATED IN MARKCTR
024639,003524:                                                                                                  #        MAGNITUDE OF POSITION DEVIATION (FOR DISPLAY) IN R22DISP METERS B-29
024640,003525:                                                                                                  #        MAGNITUDE OF VELOCITY DEVIATION (FOR DISPLAY) IN R22DISP +2 M/CSEC B-7
024641,003526:                                                                                                  #        UPDATED W-MATRIX
024642,003527: 
024643,003528:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED:
024644,003529:                                                                                                  #        LM AND CSM STATE VECTORS
024645,003530:                                                                                                  #        W-MATRIX
024646,003531:                                                                                                  #        MARK TIME IN MKTIME
024647,003532:                                                                                                  #        RADAR RANGE IN RM METERS B-29
024648,003533:                                                                                                  #                RANGE RATE IN RDOTM METERS/CSES B-7
024649,003534:                                                                                                  #                SHAFT ANGLE IN RRSHAFT REVS. B0
024650,003535:                                                                                                  #                TRUNNION ANGLE IN RRTRUN REVS. B0
024651,003536:                                                                                                  #        GIMBAL ANGLES   INNER IN AIG
024652,003537:                                                                                                  #                        MIDDLE IN AMG
024653,003538:                                                                                                  #                        OUTER IN ACG
024654,003539:                                                                                                  #        REFSMMAT
024655,003540:                                                                                                  #        RENDWFLG
024656,003541:                                                                                                  #        NOANGFLG
024657,003542:                                                                                                  #        VEHUPFLG
024658,003543: 
024659,003544:                                                                                                  #  DEBRIS:
024660,003545:                                                                                                  #        PUSHLIST -- ALL
024661,003546:                                                                                                  #        MX, MY, MZ (VECTORS)
024662,003547:                                                                                                  #  Page 575
024663,003548:                                                                                                  #        ULC, RXZ, SINTHETA, LGRET, RDRET, BVECTOR, W.IND, X78T
024664,003549: 
024665,003550: 13,2207                                           BANK     13

025056,003941: 
025057,003942:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION:
025058,003943:                                                                                                  #        LSR22.4 IS THE ENTRY TO PERFORM LUNAR SURFACE NAVIGATION FOR THE LM
025059,003944:                                                                                                  #        COMPUTER ONLY.  THIS ROUTINE COMPUTES THE BE-VECTORS AND DELTA Q FOR RANGE
025060,003945:                                                                                                  #        AND RANGE RATE MEASURED BY THE RENDEZVOUS RADAR
025061,003946: 
025062,003947:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED:
025063,003948:                                                                                                  #        INTSTALL        LGCUPDTE        INCORP1         RP-TO-R
025064,003949:                                                                                                  #        INTEGRV         GETULC          INCORP2
025065,003950: 
025066,003951:                                                                                                  #  OUTPUT
025067,003952:                                                                                                  #        CORRECTED CSM STATE VECTOR (PERMANENT)
025068,003953:                                                                                                  #        NUMBER OF MARKS INCORPORATED IN MARKCTR
025069,003954:                                                                                                  #  Page 583
025070,003955:                                                                                                  #        MAGNITUDE OF POSITION DEVIATION (FOR DISPLAY) IN R22 DISP METERS B-29
025071,003956:                                                                                                  #        MAGNITUDE OF VELOCITY DEVIATION (FOR DISPLAY) IN R22DISP +2 M/CSEC B-7
025072,003957:                                                                                                  #        UPDATED W-MATRIX
025073,003958: 
025074,003959:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED

025076,003961:                                                                                                  #        W-MATRIX
025077,003962:                                                                                                  #        MARK TIME IN MKTIME
025078,003963:                                                                                                  #        RADAR RANGE IN RM METERS B-29
025079,003964:                                                                                                  #        RANGE RATE IN RDOTM METERS/CSEC B-7
025080,003965:                                                                                                  #        VEHUPFLG

025211,004096: 26,3355           20201                                    0,1                                   
025212,004097: 26,3356           24045                           STOVL    36D                                   #  ULC IN PD0 AND MPAC,RLC IN 36D
025213,004098: 26,3357           03724                                    ULC                                   
025214,004099: 26,3360           77616                           RVQ                                            
025215,004100: 
025216,004101:                                                                                                  #  RADARANG
025217,004102: 
025218,004103:                                                                                                  #  THIS SUBROUTINE COMPUTS SINTHETA = -ULC DOT MY
025219,004104:                                                                                                  #  RXZ = (SQRT (1-SINTHETA**2))RLC
025220,004105:                                                                                                  #  OUTPUT
025221,004106:                                                                                                  #        ULC IN ULC, PD0
025222,004107:                                                                                                  #  Page 586
025223,004108:                                                                                                  #        RLC IN PD36D
025224,004109:                                                                                                  #        SIN THETA IN SINTHETA AND PD6
025225,004110:                                                                                                  #        RXZ NORM IN RXZ (N IN X1)
025226,004111: 
025227,004112: 26,3361           45020        RADARANG           STQ      CALL                                  
025228,004113: 26,3362           03675                                    RDRET                                 
025229,004114: 26,3363           55333                                    GETULC

025233,004118: 26,3367           03732                           STORE    SINTHETA

025236,004121: 26,3372           41366                           SQRT     DMP                                   
025237,004122: 26,3373           00045                                    36D                                   
025238,004123: 26,3374           60352                           SL1      NORM                                  
025239,004124: 26,3375           00047                                    X1                                    #  SET SHIFT COUNTER IN X1
025240,004125: 26,3376           03722                           STORE    RXZ                                   
025241,004126: 26,3377           77650                           GOTO                                           #  EXIT
025242,004127: 26,3400           03675                                    RDRET                                 
025243,004128: 26,3401           45020        LGCUPDTE           STQ      CALL                                  
025244,004129: 26,3402           03675                                    LGRET                                 
025245,004130: 26,3403           46531                                    INCORP1                               
025246,004131: 26,3404           51575                           VLOAD    ABVAL

025250,004135: 26,3410           56174                                    2,2                                   #  SET VEL DISPLAY TO B-7

025271,004156: 26,3435           00103 03370  IMUVAR             2DEC     E-6        B12                        #  RAD**2
025272,004157: 
025273,004158: 26,3437           00241        WSIZE              DEC      161        B-14                       
025274,004159:                                                                                                  #  Page 587
025275,004160: 26,3440           31103 36652  2PI/8              2DEC     3.141592653 B-2

025277,004162: 26,3442  E7,1456                                  EBANK=   LOSCOUNT                              
025278,004163:                                                                                                  #  Page 588
025279,004164: 
025280,004165:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME LRS24.1          RR SEARCH ROUTINE
025281,004166:                                                                                                  #  MCD NO. 0                     BY P. VOLANTE, SDC              DATE 1-15-67
025282,004167: 
025283,004168:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION
025284,004169: 
025285,004170:                                                                                                  #  DRIVES THE RENDEZVOUS RADAR IN A HEXAGONAL SEARCH PATTERN ABOUT THE LOS TO THE CSM (COMPUTED FROM THE CSM AND LM
025286,004171:                                                                                                  #  STATE VECTORS) CHECKING FOR THE DATA GOOD DISCRETE AND MONITORING THE ANGLE BETWEEN THE RADAR BORESIGHT AND THE
025287,004172:                                                                                                  #  LM +Z AXIS.  IF THIS ANGLE EXCEEDS 30 DEGREES THE PREFERRED TRACKING ATTITUDE ROUTINE IS CALLED TO PERFORM AN
025288,004173:                                                                                                  #  ATTITUDE MANEUVER.
025289,004174: 
025290,004175:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE -- BANKCALL FOR LRS24.1
025291,004176: 
025292,004177:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED
025293,004178: 
025294,004179:                                                                                                  #        LEMCONIC        R61LEM
025295,004180:                                                                                                  #        CSMCONIC        RRDESSM
025296,004181:                                                                                                  #        JOBDELAY        FLAGDOWN
025297,004182:                                                                                                  #        WAITLIST        FLAGUP
025298,004183:                                                                                                  #        RRNB            BANKCALL
025299,004184: 
025300,004185:                                                                                                  #  EXIT -- TO ENDOFJOB WHEN THE SEARCH FLAG (SRCHOPT) IS NOT SET
025301,004186: 
025302,004187:                                                                                                  #  OUTPUT
025303,004188: 
025304,004189:                                                                                                  #        DATAGOOD (SP) -- FOR DISPLAY IN R1 --   00000 INDICATES NO LOCKON
025305,004190:                                                                                                  #                                                11111 INDICATES LOCKON ACHIEVED
025306,004191:                                                                                                  #        OMEGAD (SP)   -- FOR DISPLAY IN R2 --   ANGLE BETWEEN RR BORESIGNT VECTOR AND THE SPACECRAFT +Z AXIS
025307,004192: 
025308,004193:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED:
025309,004194: 
025310,004195:                                                                                                  #        SEARCH FLAG MUST BE SET
025311,004196:                                                                                                  #        LM AND CSM STATE VECTORS AND REFSMMAT MATRIX
025312,004197: 
025313,004198:                                                                                                  #  DEBRIS
025314,004199: 
025315,004200:                                                                                                  #        RLMSRCH         UXVECT
025316,004201:                                                                                                  #        VXRLM           UYVECT
025317,004202:                                                                                                  #        LOSDESRD        NSRCHPNT
025318,004203:                                                                                                  #        DATAGOOD        OMEGAD
025319,004204:                                                                                                  #        MPAC            PUSHLIST
025320,004205: 
025321,004206: 26,3442                                           COUNT*   $$/LRS24                              
025322,004207: 26,3442           34755        LRS24.1            CAF      ZERO                                  
025323,004208: 26,3443           55736                           TS       NSRCHPNT                              #  SET SEARCH PATTERN POINT COUNTER TO ZERO
025324,004209: 26,3444           34736        CHKSRCH            CAF      BIT14                                 #  ISSUE AUTO TRACK ENABLE TO RADAR
025325,004210: 26,3445           00006                           EXTEND                                         
025326,004211:                                                                                                  #  Page 589
025327,004212: 26,3446           05012                           WOR      CHAN12                                
025328,004213: 26,3447           34736                           CAF      SRCHOBIT                              #  CHECK IF SEARCH STILL REQUESTED
025329,004214: 26,3450           70076                           MASK     FLAGWRD2                              #  (SRCHOPT FLAG SET)
025330,004215: 26,3451           00006                           EXTEND                                         
025331,004216: 26,3452           15155                           BZF      ENDOFJOB                              #  NO-TERMINATE JOB
025332,004217: 
025333,004218: 26,3453           33713                           CAF      6SECONDS                              #  SCHEDULE TASK TO DRIVE RADAR TO NEXT PT.
025334,004219: 26,3454           00004                           INHINT

025336,004221: 26,3456  E7,1456                                  EBANK=   LOSCOUNT

025533,004418: 
025534,004419:                                                                                                  #  Page 594
025535,004420:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME: R29     (RENDEZVOUS RADAR DESIGNATE DURING POWERED FLIGHT)
025536,004421:                                                                                                  #  MOD NO. 2     BY H. BLAIR-SMITH       JULY 2, 1968
025537,004422: 
025538,004423:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION:
025539,004424: 
025540,004425:                                                                                                  #        DESIGNATES THE RENDEZVOUS RADAR TOWARD THE COMPUTES LOS TO THE CSM, WITH THE CHIEF OBJECTIVE OF OBTAINING RANGE
025541,004426:                                                                                                  #        AND RANGE RATE DATA AT 2-SECOND INTERVALS FOR TRANSMISSION TO THE GROUND.  WHEN THE RR IS WITHIN .5 DEGREE OF
025542,004427:                                                                                                  #        THE COMPUTED LOS, TRACKING IS ENABLED, AND DESIGNATION CONTINUES UNTIL THE DATA-GOOD DISCRETE IS RECEIVED.  AT
025543,004428:                                                                                                  #        THAT POINT, DESIGNATION CEASES AND A RADAR-READING ROUTINE TAKES OVER, PREPARING A CONSISTENT SET OF DATA FOR
025544,004429:                                                                                                  #        DOWN TELEMETRY.  THE SET INCLUDES RANGE, RANGE RATE, MARK TIME, TWO RR CDU ANGLES, THREE IMUCDU ANGLES, AND AN
025545,004430:                                                                                                  #        INDICATOR WHICH IS 1 WHEN THE SET IS CONSISTENT AND 0 OTHERWISE.  THE INDICATOR IS IN TRKMKCNT.
025546,004431: 
025547,004432:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE:  BEGUN EVERY 2 SECONDS AS AN INTEGRAL PART OF SERVICER
025548,004433: 
025549,004434:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED:
025550,004435: 
025551,004436:                                                                                                  #        REMODE          RRPONLY
025552,004437:                                                                                                  #        UNIT            MPACVBUF
025553,004438:                                                                                                  #        QUICTRIG        AX*SR*T
025554,004439:                                                                                                  #        SPSIN           SPCOS
025555,004440:                                                                                                  #        SETRRECR        RROUT
025556,004441:                                                                                                  #        RRRDOT          RRRANGE
025557,004442: 
025558,004443:                                                                                                  #  EXIT:  TO NOR29NOW, IN SERVICER.
025559,004444: 
025560,004445:                                                                                                  #  OUTPUT:  (ALL FOR DOWNLINK)
025561,004446: 
025562,004447:                                                                                                  #        RM              RDOTM           (RAW)
025563,004448:                                                                                                  #        AIG             AMG             
025564,004449:                                                                                                  #        AOG             TRKMKCNT        TRKMKCNT = 00001 IF SET IS CONSISTENT,
025565,004450:                                                                                                  #        TANGNB          TANGNB +1       OTHERWISE TRKMKCNT = 00000.
025566,004451:                                                                                                  #        MKTIME
025567,004452:                                                                                                  #  Page 595
025568,004453: 
025569,004454:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED:
025570,004455: 
025571,004456:                                                                                                  #        NOR29FLG        READRFLG                (TO 1 AND 0 BY FRESH START) (RESET NOR29FLG TO LET SERVICER RUN R29)
025572,004457:                                                                                                  #        PIPTIME         RADMODES (BIT 10)       (BIT SET TO 0 BY FRESH START)
025573,004458:                                                                                                  #        R(CSM)          V(CSM)
025574,004459:                                                                                                  #        R               V                       (PIPTIME THRU V BY AVE G IN SERVICER)
025575,004460: 
025576,004461:                                                                                                  #  DEBRIS:
025577,004462: 
025578,004463:                                                                                                  #        RADMODES (BIT 10)
025579,004464:                                                                                                  #        LOSSM           LOSVDT/4                (= RRTARGET & LOSVEL)
025580,004465:                                                                                                  #        SAVECDUT        OLDESFLG                (SAVECDUT = MLOSV)
025581,004466:                                                                                                  #        LOSCMFLG        READRFLG
025582,004467: 
025583,004468:                                                                                                  #  ALARMS:  NONE.
025584,004469: 
025585,004470:                                                                                                  #  COMPONENT JOBS AND TASKS:
025586,004471: 
025587,004472:                                                                                                  #        INITIALIZING, IF RR IS FOUND TO BE IN MODE 1:  JOB R29REMOJ AND TASK REMODE:  ALWAYS: TASK PREPOS29.
025588,004473:                                                                                                  #        DESIGNATING:  TASK BEGDES29 & JOB R29DODES.
025589,004474:                                                                                                  #        RADAR READING:  TASK R29READ AND JOB R29RDJOB.  ALL JOBS ARE NOVAC TYPE.
025590,004475: 
025591,004476: 33,2045                                           BANK     33                                    
025592,004477: 33,2000                                           SETLOC   R29/SERV                              
025593,004478: 33,2000                                           BANK

025598,004483:

025600,004485:                                                                                                  #  SERVICER COMES TO R29 FROM "R29?" IF NOR29FLG, READRFLG, RRREMODE, RRCDUZRO, RRREPOS, AND DISPLAY-INERTIAL-DATA
025601,004486:                                                                                                  #  ARE ALL RESET, AND THE RR IS IN LGC MODE (OFTEN CONFUSINGLY CALLED AUTO MODE).

025764,004649:                                                                                                  #  Page 600
025765,004650:                                                                                                  #  R29DODES:  RR DESIGNATION LOOP FOR R29
025766,004651: 
025767,004652:                                                                                                  #  THIS ROUTINE DOES MUCH THE SAME THING AS DODES, BUT A GREAT DEAL FASTER.  IT TAKES THE NON-UNITIZED LOS VECTOR
025768,004653:                                                                                                  #  IN STABLE MEMBER COORDINATES (LOSSM) AND A DELTA-LOS IN SM AXES (LOSVDT/4) WHICH IS 1/2 SEC TIMES LOS VELOCITY,
025769,004654:                                                                                                  #  AND DEVELOPS THE SHAFT AND TRUNNION COMMANDS USING SINGLE PRECISION AS MUCH AS POSSIBLE, AND INTERPRETIVE NOT AT
025770,004655:                                                                                                  #  ALL.  THE UNIT(LOSM + LOSVEL * 1 SEC) IS COMPUTED IN DP AND TRANSFORMED TO NAV BASE COORDINATES IN DOUBLE PRE-
025771,004656:                                                                                                  #  CISION (USING SP SINES AND COSINES OF CDU ANGLES), AND THE REST IS DONE IN SP.
025772,004657: 
025773,004658:                                                                                                  #  THE FUNCTIONAL DIFFERENCE IS THAT R29DODES ALWAYS CLEARS LOSCMFLG WHEN IT ENDS, AND IT STARTS UP THE R29READ
025774,004659:                                                                                                  #  TASK WHEN LOCK-ON IS ACHIEVED.
025775,004660: 
025776,004661: 32,2547                                           BANK     32                                    
025777,004662: 32,2000                                           SETLOC   F2DPS*32                              
025778,004663: 32,2000                                           BANK                                           
025779,004664: 
025780,004665: 32,2547                                           COUNT*   $$/R29                                
025781,004666: 32,2547  E3,1760                                  EBANK=   LOSVDT/4                              
025782,004667: 
025783,004668: 32,2547           34753        R29DODES           CA       ONE                                   
025784,004669: 32,2550           55107                           TS       TANG                                  #  INDICATE 1ST PASS THRU VECTOR LOOP.
025785,004670: 32,2551           34756                           CA       FIVE                                  
025786,004671: 
025787,004672: 32,2552           10000        R29DVBEG           CCS      A                                     #  COUNT DOWN BY TWO'S IN VECTOR LOOP.
025788,004673: 32,2553           54002                           TS       Q                                     
025789,004674: 32,2554           11107                           CCS      TANG                                  
025790,004675: 32,2555           12563                           TCF      R29DPAS1                              #  DO THIS ON 1ST PASS THRU LOOP.
025791,004676: 
025792,004677: 32,2556           00006                           EXTEND                                         #  (A "PASS" HERE MEANS 3 TIMES AROUND).
025793,004678: 32,2557           50002                           INDEX    Q                                     
025794,004679: 32,2560           31761                           DCA      LOSVDT/4                              
025795,004680: 32,2561           50002                           INDEX    Q                                     
025796,004681: 32,2562           21102                           DAS      LOSSM                                 #  ADVANCE LOS VECTOR 1/2 SECOND.
025797,004682: 
025798,004683: 32,2563           00006        R29DPAS1           EXTEND                                         
025799,004684: 32,2564           50002                           INDEX    Q                                     
025800,004685: 32,2565           31102                           DCA      LOSSM                                 
025801,004686: 32,2566           50002                           INDEX    Q                                     #  MOVE CURRENT LOS (1ST PASS) OR LOS PRO-
025802,004687: 32,2567           52156                           DXCH     MPAC       +1                         #  JECTED 1/2 SEC AHEAD (2ND PASS).
025803,004688: 32,2570           11107                           CCS      TANG                                  
025804,004689: 32,2571           12577                           TCF      R29DVEND                              #  BUG OUT HERE IN 1ST PASS.
025805,004690: 
025806,004691: 32,2572           00006                           EXTEND                                         
025807,004692: 32,2573           50002                           INDEX    Q                                     
025808,004693: 32,2574           31761                           DCA      LOSVDT/4                              
025809,004694: 32,2575           50002                           INDEX    Q                                     
025810,004695: 32,2576           20156                           DAS      MPAC       +1                         #  PROJECT LOS 1 SECOND AHEAD (2ND PASS).
025811,004696: 
025812,004697: 32,2577           10002        R29DVEND           CCS      Q                                     
025813,004698: 32,2600           12552                           TCF      R29DVBEG                              #  BRANCH TO CONTINUE VECTOR LOOP.
025814,004699: 
025815,004700:                                                                                                  #  Page 601
025816,004701:                                                                                                  #  UNITIZE AND TRANSFORM TO NAV BASE AXES THE PRESENT LOS (1ST PASS) OR THE 1-SEC PROJECTED LOS (2ND PASS).
025817,004702: 
025818,004703: 32,2601           52156                           DXCH     MPAC       +1                         
025819,004704: 32,2602           52155                           DXCH     MPAC                                  
025820,004705: 32,2603           32774                           CA       R29FXLOC                              #  = ADRES INTB15 + -34D
025821,004706: 32,2604           54120                           TS       FIXLOC                                
025822,004707: 32,2605           04713                           TC       USPRCADR                              #  WITH FIXLOC ARMED FOR LENGTH AND LENGTH
025823,004708: 32,2606           01023                           CADR     UNIT                                  #  SQUARED, BORROW UNITIZING ROUTINE.
025824,004709: 32,2607           07532                           TC       MPACVBUF                              #  MOVE UNIT(LOS) TO AX*SR*T ARG AREA.
025825,004710:
